                        rightTab-cas_cit35R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">35</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Elucidating the origins of phase transformation hysteresis during electrochemical cycling of Li-Sb electrodes</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Chang, Donghee; Huo, Hua; Johnston, Karen E.; Menetrier, Michel; Monconduit, Laure; Grey, Clare P.; Van der Ven, Anton</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Journal of Materials Chemistry A: Materials for Energy and Sustainability</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2015</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">3</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">37</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">18928-18943</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">JMCAET</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">2050-7496</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Royal Society of Chemistry</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">We investigate the origins of phase transformation hysteresis in electrodes of Li-ion batteries, focusing on the alloying reaction of Li with Sb.  Electrochem. measurements confirm that the reaction path followed during Li insertion into Sb electrodes differs from that followed upon subsequent Li extn.  Results from first-principles calcns. and NMR measurements indicate that Li3Sb is capable of tolerating high Li-vacancy concns.  An unusually high Li mobility in Li3Sb facilitates over potentials during charging, which leads to a substantially larger driving force for the nucleation of Sb compared to that of Li2Sb.  The differences in nucleation driving forces arise from a lever effect that favors phases with large changes in Li concn. over phases that are closer in compn. along the equil. path.  These properties provide an explanation for the obsd. path hysteresis between charge and discharge in the Li-Sb system and likely also play a role in intercalation compds. and other alloying reactions exhibiting similar phase transformation hysteresis.</div></div></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref36"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref36" class="rightTabRefNumLink">36</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit36" data-doi="10.1515/zpch-1937-3725"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Brauer, G.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Zintl, F.</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">Z.         </div><div class="casAbstract">The structural changes in Si, electrochem. lithiated and de-lithiated at room temp., were studied by x-ray powder diffraction.  Cryst. Si becomes amorphous during Li insertion, confirming previous studies.  Highly lithiated amorphous Si suddenly crystallizes at 50 mV to form a new Li-Si phase, identified as Li15Si4.  This phase is the fully lithiated phase for Si at room temp., not Li21Si5 as is widely believed.  De-lithiation of the Li15Si4 phase produced amorphous Si.                         rightTab-cas_cit46R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">46</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Local structure of nanoporous carbons</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Petkov, V.; DiFrancesco, R. G.; Billinge, S. J. L.; Acharya, M.; Foley, H. C.</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Philosophical Magazine B: Physics of Condensed Matter: Statistical Mechanics, Electronic, Optical and Magnetic Properties</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">1999</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">79</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">10</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">1519-1530</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">PMABDJ</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">0958-6644</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Taylor &amp; Francis Ltd.</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">The local at. structure of nanoporous carbons produced by pyrolysis of poly(furfuryl alc.) at various temps. has been studied using neutron diffraction.  At. pair distribution functions (PDFs) were obtained from the neutron data.  Structure models have been fitted to the PDFs to understand the fine features of at. ordering.  It has been found that carbons produced at 800 and 1200°C are made of stacked graphene sheets, that are more or less curved.  The 400°C-processed carbon has a heavily distorted nonplanar structure.  For each sample we have detd. the extent of the structural coherence, the av. d. within the structurally coherent regions and the proportion of carbon atoms, which are trigonally coordinated.  Microscopic models were also produced for the local structure of the nanoporous carbons investigated.</div></div></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref47"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref47" class="rightTabRefNumLink">47</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit47" data-doi="10.1016/j.jpowsour.2015.01.093"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Saubanère, M.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Yahia, M.-B.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Lemoigno, F.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Doublet, M.-L.</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">J. Power Sources</span><span class="NLM_x"> </span><span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2015</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_volume">280</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_fpage">695</span><span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1016/j.jpowsour.2015.01.093</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord empty" id="
                            rightTab-cas_R
                        "><div class="casContent">There is no corresponding record for this reference.</div></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref48"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref48" class="rightTabRefNumLink">48</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit48" data-doi="10.1021/nl502812x"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Kohandehghan, A.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Cui, K.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Kupsta, M.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Ding, J.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Memarzadeh Lotfabad, E.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Kalisvaart, W. P.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Milin, D.</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">Nano Lett.</span><span class="NLM_x"> </span><span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2014</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_volume">14</span><span class="NLM_x"> (</span><span class="NLM_issue">10</span><span class="NLM_x">) </span> <span class="NLM_fpage">5873</span><span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1021/nl502812x</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord empty" id="
                            rightTab-cas_R
                        "><div class="casContent">There is no corresponding record for this reference.</div></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref49"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref49" class="rightTabRefNumLink">49</a></strong><div class="note"><p class="first last">Note that the scale factor for the a-Na<sub>1.7</sub>Sb phase during S2-b is less than 1 because approximately 30–40% of the antimony is still present as c-Sb. When doing the linear combination fitting, the PDF for a-Na<sub>1.7</sub>Sb was scaled by 1.17 to account for that fact that at the end of D1-a only approximately 85% of the electrode was present as a-Na<sub>1.7</sub>Sb—some c-Na<sub>3</sub>Sb still remained.</p></div><div class="citationLinks"><div class="casRecord empty" id="
                            rightTab-cas_R
                        "><div class="casContent">There is no corresponding record for this reference.</div></div></div></div></li></ol></li><li id="pane-m3" aria-labelledby="pane-m3" class="tab__pane tab__pane-suppInfo"><h2 class="supp-info-label">Supporting Information</h2><div class="article_supporting-info" id="rightTab-notes-1"><div class="article_content-header"><div class="article_content-header-row"><div class="article_content-title" tabindex="0"><h2 id="rightTab-_i23">Supporting Information</h2></div></div></div><hr><p class="last">The Supporting Information is available free of charge on the <a href="/" class="ext-link">ACS Publications website</a> at DOI: <a href="/doi/abs/10.1021/jacs.5b13273" class="ext-link">10.1021/jacs.5b13273</a>.</p><ul class="NLM_list-list_type-label" id="silist"><li><p class="inline">Full PDF data, further details about XRD and PDF analysis, DFT calculations and 2D NMR results. (<a href="/doi/suppl/10.1021/jacs.5b13273/suppl_file/ja5b13273_si_001.pdf" class="ext-link">PDF</a>)</p></li></ul><p></p><div class="supInfoBoxOnFTP "><div class="sup-info-attachments"><ul><li><a class="suppl-anchor" href="/doi/suppl/10.1021/jacs.5b13273/suppl_file/ja5b13273_si_001.pdf">ja5b13273_si_001.pdf (4.61 MB)</a></li></ul></div></div><div id="rightTab-figshare-widget"></div><br><div class="TermsAndConditionsDropzoneRight" data-pb-dropzone="TermsAndConditionsDropzoneRight"><div data-widget-def="UX3HTMLWidget" data-widget-id="b84e6b6c-b4d0-4427-b286-3cf14d52d013" class="mb-4">

        <script nonce="9318af6d3abc88d3-SJC">
(function(){
	
	/*Event Tracking for RIS menu dropdown - Article pages*/

	$('.cit-download-dropdown_button').on('click',function(e)
	{	
		e.preventDefault();
	    gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':'Main'});

	});


	$('.cit-download-dropdown_content ul li').on('click',function(e)
	{	
	//	e.preventDefault();
	    var idx = $(this).index();
	    
	    var label = '';
	    if (idx === 0 ) {
	    	label = 'Citation';
	    } else if (idx === 1 ) {
	    	label = 'Abstract';
	    } else if (idx === 2 ) {
	    	label = 'Reference';
	    } else if (idx === 3 ) {
	    	label = 'More Options';
	    }
	   
	   gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':label});
	});

	$('.header_contnav-next a').on('click', function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Right Arrow'});
	}); 

 	$('.header_contnav-pre a').on('click', function(e){
	    e.preventDefault();
	     gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Left Arrow'});
	}); 

	$('.share_button').on('click', function(e){
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Share'});
	});

	$("#pane-m1con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Figures'});
	});

	$("#pane-m2con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
	    gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'References'});
	});

	$("#pane-m3con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Supporting Info'});
	});

	$('.tab__close').on('click', function(){
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Close'});
	}); 



})();

</script>

<script nonce="9318af6d3abc88d3-SJC">
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    const modalContainer = document.querySelector('.my-main-container');

    // Function to show the modal
    function showModal() {
        modalContainer.style.display = 'flex';
        document.querySelector('.overlay').style.display = 'block';
    }

    // Function to hide the modal when the close button is clicked
    function hideModal() {
        modalContainer.style.display = 'none';
        document.querySelector('.overlay').style.display = 'none';
    }

    // Hide the modal initially
    hideModal();

    // Function to handle clicks outside the modal
    function handleClickOutside(event) {
        // const modalContainer = document.querySelector(".my-main-container");
        // Check if the click target is not a child of the modal container
        if (!modalContainer.contains(event.target)) {
            hideModal();
        }
    }

    // Add a click event listener to the close button
    document
        .querySelector('.close-button')
        .addEventListener('click', hideModal);

    // Add a click event listener to the document to handle clicks outside the modal
    document.addEventListener('click', handleClickOutside);

    const screenHeight = window.innerHeight;
    function updateModalPosition() {
        const scrollY = window.scrollY;
        // console.log("scrollY= " + scrollY);
        // modalContainer.style.top = `${50 + scrollY}px`;
        modalContainer.style.top = `${scrollY + screenHeight / 2}px`;
        // console.log("new top= " + modalContainer.style.top);
    }

    // Update the modal position when the user scrolls
    window.addEventListener('scroll', updateModalPosition);

    // Initialize the modal position
    updateModalPosition();

    //---Cookie---
    // Function to set the cookie with a given name, value, and expiration time in days
    function setCookie(name, value, days) {
        var expires = '';
        if (days) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime() + days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
            expires = '; expires=' + date.toUTCString();
            console.log(expires + 'this is expires dateUTC');
        }
        document.cookie = name + '=' + (value || '') + expires + '; path=/';
        // console.log("document.cookie is: " + document.cookie);
    }

    if (!document.cookie.includes('modalAd')) {
        // Show Modal
        showModal();

        // Set the cookie with the name "modalAd", value "true", and expiration of 3 day
        setCookie('modalAd', 'true', 3);
    } else {
        hideModal();
    }
});

</script>

<script nonce="9318af6d3abc88d3-SJC">
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(){
    // Function to get a Human readable formatted date
    function getFormattedDateForMaintenance() {
        let today = new Date();
        let dd = String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
        //January is 0
        let mm = String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0'); 
        let yyyy = today.getFullYear();
        
        let daysOfWeek = ['Sunday', 'Monday', 'Tuesday', 'Wednesday', 'Thursday', 'Friday', 'Saturday'];
        let monthsOfYear = ['January', 'February', 'March', 'April', 'May', 'June', 'July', 'August', 'September', 'October', 'November', 'December'];

        let dayOfWeek = daysOfWeek[today.getDay()];
        let monthOfYear = monthsOfYear[today.getMonth()];

        return dayOfWeek + ', ' + monthOfYear + ' ' + dd + ', ' + yyyy;
    }
    
    // Insert the date into the .system-message-date element
    document.querySelector('.system-message-date').innerText = getFormattedDateForMaintenance();
});
</script>

        $("#gdpr-message-modal").show();
      }

      function handleClick() {
        //console.log($("#gdpr-input").val());
        emailValid = validateEmail($("#gdpr-input").val());
        if (emailValid) {
          //Submit the form
          //Hide form
          if ($(".gdpr_err")) {
            $(".gdpr_err").hide();
          }

          $("#gdpr-message-content");
          //If successful then...
          setCookie("gdpr", "true");
          //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid + " submiting form");
        } else {
          //Show error message
          gdprErrorMessage();
          //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid);
        }
      }

      function gdprErrorMessage() {
        if (errorStatus) {
          return false;
        } else {
          errorStatus = true;
          $("#gdpr-message-content").append(errormessage);
        }
      }

      function validateEmail(email) {
        var re =
          /^(([^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+(\.[^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+)*)|(".+"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
        return re.test(String(email).toLowerCase());
      }

      function setCookie(name, value) {
        var expires = "";
        expires = "; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT";
        document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "") + expires + "; path=/";
      }

      function getCookie(name) {
        var match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp(name + "=([^;]+)"));
        if (match) return match[1];
      }

      function hideForm() {
        //And set cookie
        $("#gdpr-message-modal").hide();
        setCookie("gdpr", "false");
        gtag("event", "GDPR Modal", {
          event_category: "Pubs GDPR",
          event_label: "GDPR Dismissal",
        });
      }

      return {
        init: init,
      };
    })();

    $(document).ready(infoCentralCapture.init);
  </script>
</p>
-->

                    
                        



        
        <script nonce="9318af6d3abc88d3-SJC">
var currentJournal = "Journal of the American Chemical Society";
$(".citationLinks > a").click(function(e){
    if($(this).text() === "ACS Full Text ") {
        gtag('event', 'ACS Full Text', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Crossref") {
        gtag('event', 'Crossref', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "CAS") {
        gtag('event', 'CAS', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "PubMed") {
        gtag('event', 'PubMed', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Google Scholar") {
        gtag('event', 'Google Scholar', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).hasClass("issue-item_open-url") === true) {
        gtag('event', 'OpenURL', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
});
</script>
